###########################
# 2) Server configuration #
###########################
com.bank.BankServer.aliveMsgPeriod = 2000
com.bank.BankServer.gracePeriodMultiplier = 50
com.bank.BankServer.startupdelay.Citi_1 = 80000	//START LATE
com.bank.BankServer.startupdelay.Citi_2 = 0
com.bank.BankServer.startupdelay.Citi_3 = 160000 //START VERY LATE
com.bank.BankServer.startupdelay.Citi_4 = 0

com.bank.BankServer.dieAfterNMsg.Citi_1 = 100000
com.bank.BankServer.dieAfterNMsg.Citi_2 = 1	//DIE AFTER SOME TIME
com.bank.BankServer.dieAfterNMsg.Citi_3 = 100000
com.bank.BankServer.dieAfterNMsg.Citi_4 = 100000
com.bank.BankServer.map=Citi,Citi_1,localhost:61616/Citi,Citi_2,localhost:61616/Citi,Citi_3,localhost:61616/Citi,Citi_4,localhost:61616
############################################################################################################
1)Citi_3's dies. (internal node)
2)Citi_2's dies. (internal node)
3)Citi_3 is added.(as tail)
